\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{backend__bases_8py_source_l01606}01606\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ A\ context\ manager\ that\ allows\ terminating\ a\ plot\ by\ sending\ a\ SIGINT.\ \ It}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{backend__bases_8py_source_l01607}01607\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ is\ necessary\ because\ the\ running\ backend\ prevents\ the\ Python\ interpreter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{backend__bases_8py_source_l01608}01608\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ from\ running\ and\ processing\ signals\ (i.e.,\ to\ raise\ a\ KeyboardInterrupt).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{backend__bases_8py_source_l01611}01611\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ function\ which\ organizes\ a\ write\ of\ the\ signal\ number\ into\ a\ socketpair.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{backend__bases_8py_source_l01614}01614\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ notifier\ object,\ that\ object\ is\ kept\ alive\ while\ the\ context\ manager\ runs.)}}
